 ' centre sarkaar ne kaha he ki sibiesai or rajya bordon main saajha paathyakram pesh karne kii uski koi yojana nahin he, kyonki saajha samaan paathyakram main sthaneey sandarbh, samskruti or bhashaa ko shaamil nahin kiya ja saktaa
 Minister of State for Human Resource Development Upendra Kushwaha gave this information in the Lok Sabha in response to the questions of the members during the Question Hour
 unhone saath hi bataaya ki shiksha par rashtriya niti main saajha aadharbhoot mulyon ke saath paathyakram main ek rashtriya praaroop kaa prastaav he, jisamen swatantraaa andolan kaa itihaas, sanvaidhanik gatividhiyaan tathaa anya aisi jaruri saamagree shaamil he, jo ek rashtriya pahchaan ke poshan ke liye jaruri he
 He said that the states have agreed on the national draft
 ek anya sawaal ke likhit jawaab main maanav sansaadhan vikaas mantri prakaash jaavdekar ne bataaya ki paathyakram or shaikshanik sansadhano main bahulata vaanchit he, kyonki deshbhar main ek saajha samaan paathyakram sthaneey sandarbh, samskruti or bhashaa ko sangyaan main nahin letaa
 The comments unase sawaal kiya gaya tha ki kya sarkaar kaa sibiesai, rajya bordon or rashtriya mukt shiksha skulon tathaa bhartiya skool praaanpatr pariksha board (aiesasiibi) main saajha paathyakram pesh karne kaa koi prastaav he
 Responding to a supplementary question regarding the weight of school settlements of children, Kushwaha said that efforts are on to reduce the burden of disposal
 unhone daawa kiya ki sarkaar apane is prayaas main kaaphi safal bhi rahi he

 In the old Hindi films, we often saw that in the Kumbh Mela, children were separated from their parents or brothers
 milte milaate bhi 15 se 20 saal lag jate the
 The most interesting incident occurred when, years later, the separated were identified with a locket tied around the neck
 maa apane bete ko gale main pahane locket se pahachaanati thi yaa ek bhai duusare bhai ko gale main pahane taabeej se pahchaan letaa tha
 Now that talk of Hindi films has become old
 bhale hi prayagraj kumbh main lakhon karodon kii bheed aa rahi ho, lekin is baar aapke apane aap se nahin bichhadenge
 Because this time, your younger brother or children are being given amulets in the Kumbh Mela, which will make it easy to identify the lost ones
 ji haa yah 2019 kaa aadhunik taabeej he jo kumbh main hue apano ko ek duusare se milwa degaa
 3 Khoya Paaya Centers built in the Sangam area, in fact, this time on the Mahadarva of Ardh Kumbha in Prayagraj, the usual Khoya Paaya centers have been built in the midst of modern preparations, but for the first time these Khoya Paaya centers are looking very modern
 yogi sarkaar kii ore se akele sangam ilaake main 3 khoyaa paaya centre banaae gaye hai, jahaan aane vaale shraddhalu bichade hue logon ke bare main jaankaree de sakate hai or vahiin se ghoshnaa kii jaati he, jisase apano ko dhundne main madad mil sake, lekin usase bhi jabardast or behtareen vyavastha us jaadui aadhunik taabeej kii he jo chote bacchon ke gale main pahanaai ja rahi he
 The card is hung around the neck of the children
 Modern amulet is equipped with RFID technology, through which young children are registered as soon as they come to the Kumbh Mela and hang a card like a swap card around their neck
 registration ke dauraan hi bacchon ke saath aae mata pita kaa phone number or unka puraa pataa darj kiya jaataa he
 All this data is fed into the card, which is worn by wrapping it in a special kind of paper around the neck of the child and putting it in a plastic cover
 card main hoti he bachche se judi ahm jaankareeis card par likhaa he kripaya meri madad karen, yani agar aapkaa baccha aapse khoyaa to kumbh meley main gum rahaa koi bhi shaks us bachche ke gale main card dekhakar use najdiki khoyaa paaya centre tak yaa khoyaa paaya centre ke sahaayak boothon tak pahunchaa degaa
 As soon as the card placed around the child's neck at that center will be placed on a special machine, an emergency message will be sent immediately to the register number of the child's parents, as well as the agent's number at the booth where the child is standing
 
 mela ilaake main 6 hitech rfidi khoyaa paaya boothis rfidi takanic ko pehali baar kumbh meley main istemaal kiya ja rahaa he
 Sanjay Pandey, who put RFID tags in children during registration at Khoya Paaya Center, says that with this technology, children will no longer be lost in the fair and if they are lost, it will be very easy to locate them
 mela ilaake main aise hitech rfidi khoyaa paaya booth philhal chah sthapit kiye gaye hai
